  3016. # [19:32] <bz> 51 * By default a timer will fire on the thread that created it. Set the .target
  3017. # [19:32] <bz> 52 * attribute to fire on a different thread. Once you have set a timer's .target
  3018. # [19:32] <bz> 53 * and called one of its init functions, any further interactions with the timer
  3019. # [19:32] <bz> 54 * (calling cancel(), changing member fields, etc) should only be done by the
  3020. # [19:32] <bz> 55 * target thread, or races may occur with bad results like timers firing after
  3021. # [19:32] <bz> 56 * they've been canceled, and/or not firing after re-initiatization.
